				<script type="text/javascript">
			$J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlay = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayBottom = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_bottom');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode = window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

											if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
							$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
							$ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn.append( $Header );
						else
							$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						{
							$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
							$Header.show();

							var nStartingScrollPosition = $J('#store_header').height();
							if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nStartingScrollPosition )
								$Window.scrollTop( nStartingScrollPosition );

							$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
						}
									} );
				
				window.setTimeout( function() { $J(window).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu'); }, 0 );

										var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						
													g_rgUserPreferences['use_store_query'] = 1;
						
						g_rgUserPreferences['use_search_spellcheck'] = 1;
						g_rgUserPreferences['search_creators_and_tags'] = 1;

						if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
						{
							// default search support where the web page includes the search edit control
							EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_5_9_', 'SG', 1, 'schinese', g_rgUserPreferences, '20235974' );
						}
						else 
						{
							// search support for the mobile client.  the mobile client has a native search edit control but relies on the web content to perform the query and show results
													}
				
				// make genre categories expand/collapse on mobile
				$J(document).on( 'click', '.popup_genre_expand_header', function ( event ) {
					if ( !UseSmallScreenMode() )
						return;

					event.preventDefault();
					var $Element = $J(this);
					var $Target = $J('.popup_genre_expand_content[data-genre-group=' + $Element.data('genre-group') + ']' );
					if ( $Element.data('group-expanded') )
					{
						$Target.slideUp();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', false );
					}
					else
					{
						$Target.slideDown();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', true );
					}
				});
			} );
		</script>

                                    <script type="text/javascript">
                                        $J( function() {
                                            var player = new HighlightPlayer( {
                                                elemPlayerArea: 'highlight_player_area',
                                                elemStrip: 'highlight_strip',
                                                elemStripScroll: 'highlight_strip_scroll',
                                                elemSlider: 'highlight_slider',
                                                rgScreenshotURLs: rgScreenshotURLs
                                            } );

                                            $J('#highlight_slider_right').click( function() {
                                                player.Transition( true );
                                            });
                                            $J('#highlight_slider_left').click( function() {
                                                player.TransitionBack( true );
                                            });

                                            
                                                // swipe gesture handling for the media carousel

                                                // TODO: We may want to move all of this to the player class so it has built in touch gesture support.
                                                // First testing here as part of new mobile ux.

                                                var k_nElementWidth = 120;
                                                var k_playerItemClassName = '.highlight_player_item';
                                                var g_nStripWidth = 1080;
                                                var g_nMediaItems = player.m_elemPlayerArea.find( '.highlight_player_item' ).length;
                                                var g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                // Handle left/right swipe on the media playback by moving forward or backward when the swipe completes
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    if ( xdiff > ydiff && ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable ) )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined ||
                                                        typeof eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX;
                                                    var ydiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY;

                                                    // clear out the touch start event
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                    // ignore the swipe if it was short and could've been intended as a tap, or the
                                                    // direction was more vertical than horizontal
                                                    if ( Math.abs( xdiff ) < 20 || Math.abs( ydiff ) > Math.abs( xdiff ) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                    // move forward or backward but don't wrap as that would be a jarring user experience
                                                    if ( xdiff > 0 )
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.next( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.Transition( true );
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.prev( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.TransitionBack( true );
                                                    }
                                                });

                                                // when the thumbnail strip is swiped move the strip at a granular level
                                                // so it feels active.  The active image does not update because when testing the code to
                                                // make it change the active element it seemed annoying
                                                var g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                var g_nMaxScroll = g_nMediaItems > 3 ? ( ( g_nMediaItems - 3 ) * k_nElementWidth ) : 0;

                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = parseInt( player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left' ) );

                                                    player.StopCycle();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    var xdiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );
                                                    if ( Math.abs(ydiff) > Math.abs(xdiff) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // move the scroll strip without changing the selected item
                                                    var nNewScrollPosition = parseInt( g_nSwipeStartingPosition + xdiff );

                                                    // check that we don't scroll past the ends
                                                    if ( nNewScrollPosition > 0 )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = 0;
                                                    else if ( nNewScrollPosition < (-1 * g_nMaxScroll) )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = (-1 * g_nMaxScroll);

                                                    // set the new scroll position
                                                    player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left', nNewScrollPosition + 'px' );

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                });

										
                                            if( window.location.hash )
                                            {
                                                var ssid = window.location.hash.substr(1);
                                                player.HighlightScreenshot(ssid);
                                            }
                                        } );
                                    </script>
                                                            </div>
                        					</div>
				</div>
				<div style="clear: both;"></div>
			</div>
			</div>

							<div class="heading">
																	<h1 class="inset">抢先体验游戏</h1>
									<h2 class="inset">立刻获取体验权限然后开始游戏，并随着游戏的发展参与其中。</h2>
									<p><span>注意：</span>该抢先体验的游戏内容尚不完整且也许会发生变化。如果您目前不是特别想玩这款游戏，那么您应该等待一段时间来观察游戏的开发进度。<a href="https://store.steampowered.com/earlyaccessfaq/?snr=1_5_9_">了解更多</a></p>
															</div>
							<div id="earlyAccessBody" class="devnotes">
																	<div class="devs_say">开发者的话：</div>
								
								<div id="devnotes_expander">
																			<h1>为何要采用抢先体验这种模式？</h1>
										“We have chosen to start with early access, because not all of our goals are yet achieved. We are still actively working on the game and want to add more features to create the perfect metaverse to enjoy for everyone at anytime. We will make avatars with custom actions and animations, worlds with custom triggers, inventories and progress saving and user created game modes possible. Everyone should be able to create game modes like tower defense, conquest, or whatever. Shooters, MMOs and many more. We want to provide templates over time so people can get this game fit to what they want to play in that specific moment.<br>
<br>
We really appreciate feedback by everyone of you on our Discord, steam discussions or via support email.<br>
<br>
We really wanna achieve all of our goals - with all of you - together.”

										<h1>这款游戏的抢先体验状态大约持续多久？</h1>
										“We will approximately leave early access 6-9 months after release (open beta).”

										<h1>计划中的完整版本和抢先体验版本到底有多少不同？</h1>
										“During early access we will further optimize and tweak performance and safety for every user.<br>
We want to deliver freedom as well as safety. Thats how a social sandbox is meant to be in our opinion. We also want to add more community focused features like the groups system, a extended friends system and more ways to customize social interaction and various game modes. We also want to add templates for game mode creation to make it more easy for players to create all the nice stuff they want to create.”

										<h1>抢先体验版本的现状如何？</h1>
										“The game is already featuring the main features as uploading content, adding friends, interacting, joining worlds and forming groups. There is also a huge backend community hub to manage every social interaction and the uploaded content in the metaverse.<br>
We run a community discord where players and developers can communicate and improve the game together.”

										<h1>在抢先体验期间和结束之后，游戏价格会有所不同吗？</h1>
										“The game is and will always be free to play. With the free account you will be able to upload up to ten avatars / worlds and will not be able to create groups. Those limits can be lifted by purchasing the account unlock.”

										<h1>在开发过程中，你们是如何计划让玩家社区参与进来的？</h1>
										“We run a bugtracker and feature requester that can be accessed by every registered user in our gate. We comment on every request telling users our opinions and ideas on the specific topics and actively add new content based on users requests.<br>
<br>
For questions and feedback you can join our discord at https://discord.gg/abi”

July\u2019s game update and subsequent issues, information for creators, and a community showcase.\n\n[h1]July Update Recap[\/h1]\nLast month, ChilloutVR released a major update that had been a work in progress for quite some time. Much was worked on during this development period to make significant improvements to the game as a whole, far more than what could be briefly mentioned here, and we\u2019ve been enamored by the positive feedback from the community.\n\nYou can read the full changelog here:\n[url=https:\/\/store.steampowered.com\/news\/app\/661130\/view\/3650781708186173693]https:\/\/store.steampowered.com\/news\/app\/661130\/view\/3650781708186173693[\/url]\n\nWhile we\u2019re very happy to take this next step forward in ChilloutVR\u2019s development, a number of bugs were found by the community soon after release that are currently being investigated. This includes issues such as lip syncing and voice chat occasionally not functioning as expected, among various other minor issues that are actively being worked on. We hope to have them resolved as soon as possible, so stay tuned for further updates.\n\n\n[h1]Shader Replacement[\/h1]\nTo recap some information we\u2019ve shared in our July Status Report, an alternative and more optimized rendering method called Single Pass Instanced was introduced during the development of Unity 2019. It was available alongside Single Pass rendering, which had been commonly used for VR game development, and is what most content uploaded to ChilloutVR was intended for. However, as of Unity 2020, Single Pass rendering is no longer supported and any projects looking to upgrade their version of Unity must also take this into consideration. This doesn\u2019t so much concern development of the game as it does creation of assets, which in our case would be Avatars, Worlds, and Props, because shaders used with uploaded content must have support for Single Pass Instanced. While some popular shaders created and used by the community have already adopted these changes to ensure future compatibility, those that haven\u2019t may only render in one eye as a result.\n\nTo remedy this, an attempt is made to replace the shader if possible, or fallback to Standard. This may not be reliable in all cases, and could cause content to not look as originally intended.\n\n[b]We urge creators to update their incompatible content as soon as possible.[\/b]\n\nThose familiar with developing shaders, or want to learn, can use Unity\u2019s documentation as a resource here:\n[url=https:\/\/docs.unity3d.com\/Manual\/SinglePassInstancing.html]https:\/\/docs.unity3d.com\/Manual\/SinglePassInstancing.html[\/url]\n\n\n\n\n[h1]Content Patching[\/h1]\nAs a result of the Unity engine upgrade, there was a major problem when loading a comparatively small number of content built with Unity 2019. Anything bundled using Audio Mixers and loaded on the latest version of ChilloutVR would often cause the game to crash, creating an unstable and uncertain environment after the update was released. An investigation concluded that it was an issue that would need to be fixed by Unity themselves, which was done in Unity 2022, but requests to backport this fix have been rejected. Unfortunately due to a number of other problems with Unity 2022, it is not a viable upgrade for ChilloutVR at this time.\n\nSo while this may not be an issue that we can directly fix ourselves, another approach was taken. Over the course of a few days, all content uploaded to ChilloutVR with Unity 2019 was scanned and subsequently patched if this particular issue was found. For those interested, here are some stats on how much content was effected:\n\n- Avatars: 11,711\n- Props: 2,707\n- Worlds: 96\n\nNew content will continue to be patched for a time, but uploading via Unity 2019 and CCK 3.4 will not be possible in the near future to prevent this and other issues from persisting.\n\nIf you have not yet upgraded your project(s) to Unity 2021 or CCK 3.5, relevant information can be found here:\n[url=https:\/\/developers.abinteractive.net\/cck\/setup\/]https:\/\/developers.abinteractive.net\/cck\/setup\/[\/url]\n\n\n[h1]r\/place[\/h1]\nOver the last few years, Reddit has hosted a collaborative event on the subreddit r\/place where individuals all across the site can all contribute towards one large canvas by placing only a single pixel every few minutes. Naturally, this has led to many communities vying to claim and maintain a spot, in addition to some stunning art, to ultimately be immortalized in the final piece.\n\nDuring the most recent event, several members of the community were able to secure a spot and spread some love for ChilloutVR. We love to see efforts like this from the community, and are really appreciative of those who take the time to show their support in various ways.\n\nCanvas: [url=https:\/\/placedata.reddit.com\/data\/final_2023_place.png]https:\/\/placedata.reddit.com\/data\/final_2023_place.png[\/url]\nLocation: Lower left corner\n\n[img]https:\/\/i.imgur.com\/BYQR7vP.png[\/img]\n\nWe hope to occasionally showcase more unique and interesting work from the community in the future, so we\u2019ll be looking out for more!\n\n\n[h1]Final Notes[\/h1]\nAs always, thank you for your continued interest and support of ChilloutVR's development.\n\nNext month, expect to hear about our future plans for the next major update of ChilloutVR. 2023r171","posttime":1690370339,"updatetime":1690370339,"body":"We have just released a new update for ChilloutVR on the stable branch.\n\n[h1]ChilloutVR 2023r171[\/h1]\n\nThis update contains the upgrade to Unity 2021. We decided to release this update earlier in order to get our update schedule back to a steady pace.\nMany other changes were held back by some issues that were introduced along with the Unity engine update. Most of those issues were the responsibility of third-party developers to resolve, which caused a setback in our schedule.\nThe most prevalent of those issues cause random crashes when loading a portion of uploaded content. This bug was reported to Unity, and subsequently fixed in recent versions, but has yet to be fixed in 2021.\nWe have a plan to work around this issue by iterating through uploaded content and patching the affected content accordingly. We are positive this will be resolved in the coming days.\n\nBy releasing the engine upgrade now, these issues are no longer preventing future releases from making it to the stable branch. As a result, updates frequency can be expected to persist now that this is no longer a problem.\n\nThis update contains the following major changes:\n\n[h2]New Voice Chat System:[\/h2]\nChilloutVR\u2019s voice chat system will be switching from Dissonance to Vivox. This fixes a number of issues experienced due to limitations of the former, such as crackling and cut-outs; whereas Vivox demonstrated much better voice quality and stability in both development and community testing, offering an improved experience for user-to-user communication\n\n[h2]Shader Replacement System:[\/h2]\nThe shaders for content that were uploaded with cck 3.3 or earlier will have their shaders replaced in VR mode.\nAn attempt is made to match the shader in question with available shaders in the game. If the shader is unknown, it will be replaced with the Standard shader.\nThis ensures that legacy content will not render in only one eye.\nContent that is uploaded after this update with incompatible shaders may still exhibit this behavior.\nIf present in a world where shaders are replaced, an appropriate icon will be displayed in the Quick Menu and World Details Page.\nMaterial swaps will most likely inhibit the Replacement System from working properly.\n\n[h2]OpenXR and SteamVR:[\/h2]\nThe Game now supports SteamVR and OpenXR. The default will continue to be SteamVR since a lot of implementations, such as Device Management and Haptics, currently work much better in SteamVR.\nThe following launch option can be used to launch the game in OpenXR Mode: --force-openxr\n\n[h2]Graphic Presets:[\/h2]\nThe Graphic menu now contains a preset option in order to make the graphics customization more accessible.\n\n[h2]Mod Network:[\/h2]\nThe Mod Network is a built-in networking layer that mod developers can utilize.\nIt allows for Mods to communicate between Users in the same instance in a secure way without needing any third-party Networking library or services.\n\n[h2]Animator Driver:[\/h2]\nThe Animator Driver is a new Component that can be added to animator states and can switch Animator Parameters on State Enter and Exit. The functionality is comparable to the Variable Buffer Arithmetic of the Interactable.\nIf used on Avatars it will sync corresponding Advanced Avatar Values. On Props, it will set the Sync values as well if the Parameter matches.\n\n[h2]Spawnable Pickup Markers:[\/h2]\nSpawnable Pickup Markers can now be placed in Worlds. They work comparably to the Avatar Pickup Marker, and are similar in design.\n\n[h2]PlayerMaterialParser:[\/h2]\nThis new component can parse the positions of players to a Vector4[255] on a specified material.\nThis component gives you access to the following positions:\n- Root\n- Hip\n- Head\n- Left Hand\n- Right Hand\n- Chest\n- Left Foot\n- Right Foot\nThe W component of Root will contain the Avatar Viewpoint height.\nThis component can be used to have shaders react to Players without the need for cameras for example water or snow.\n\n[h2]General fixes and changes:[\/h2]\n- Fixed some issues regarding depth buffer on AMD GPUs\n- Fixed a bug that lead to velocity not being transferred to the player correctly\n- Fixed an issue that lead to Compatibility Issues with some RenderTexture 									<div class="game_page_autocollapse_ctn collapsed"><div data-panel="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;PanelGroup&quot;}" id="aboutThisGame" class="game_page_autocollapse" style="max-height: 850px;">
						<div id="game_area_description" class="game_area_description">
							<h2>关于这款游戏</h2>
							Have you ever dreamt of a world where you can create and explore anything you want? ChilloutVR is a community-driven VR &amp; Desktop sandbox game supposed to enable players as well as creators to create and explore a huge metaverse.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/661130/extras/welcome.png?t=1643304966"><br><br>Welcome to ChilloutVR, your new place to be. Be able to create your own avatar or use existing avatars, explore a huge metaverse containing lots of different servers, game modes, avatars, and worlds.<br><br>The main goal of ChilloutVR is to provide a secure and performant base game for creators and players around the world.<br><br>An AlphaLink account is required to play this game. You will be asked to create this account after starting the game.<h2 class="bb_tag">Be who you want to be</h2>You can create your own Avatar, your new self in ChilloutVR. You can play as your avatar, explore worlds, meet friends, and make new friends.<h2 class="bb_tag">Be where you want to be</h2>You can be wherever you want to be, the huge community of content creators is one of the many reasons why ChilloutVR is a game that is enjoyable over a long period of time. You can explore a daily growing amount of publically available worlds alone, with friends or with people you just met. You can also open up new worlds with just a click. Visit and explore a huge amount of virtual worlds or just create your own.<br><br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/661130/extras/creative.png?t=1643304966"><h2 class="bb_tag">Avatars</h2>You are enabled to create your own, fully expressive, full-body tracked avatars with lip sync and eye-tracking. Full-body tracking is not required, VR is not required. <br>You can find more detailed information on what custom avatars can contain and what the requirements are in our documentation.<h2 class="bb_tag">Worlds</h2>You are enabled to create your own, fully immersive worlds including interactable objects.<h2 class="bb_tag">Scripting &amp; Game modes (not yet available)</h2>ChilloutVR is built modular, allowing everyone to create interactive worlds with interactable objects or even full game modes - all using our in-house scripting toolkit "Newton" (not yet available). This way we allow creators to create game modes like Trouble in Terrorist town, various kinds of coop tower defense games or even MMORPGs in ChilloutVR. The only limitation is your imagination and the players computer performance.<br><br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/661130/extras/friends.png?t=1643304966"><h2 class="bb_tag">Social interactions around the metaverse</h2>Add your friends and join them, drop portals to other instances to have them follow your way around the metaverse, join public instances to find new people, and make new friends. <br>You can also join groups to connect with other communities or spend time with the people you like.<h2 class="bb_tag">Join the party</h2>Attend events of all kinds, be a part of groups, or create your own. You are welcome to enjoy events and talks with many users online.<br><br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/661130/extras/explore.png?t=1643304966"><br><br>In ChilloutVR you can explore the many worlds of the metaverse, either alone or with your friends. When exploring online you can decide if only your friends or random people from across the world can join you in your adventures.						</div>
					</div><div class="game_page_autocollapse_fade"><div class="game_page_autocollapse_readmore">展开阅读</div></div></div>

		<h2>系统需求</h2>
				<div class="sysreq_contents">
							<div class="game_area_sys_req sysreq_content active" data-os="win">

								<strong>最低配置:</strong><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>需要 64 位处理器和操作系统<br></li><li><strong>操作系统:</strong> Windows 7 / 8 / 8.1 / 10 (x64)<br></li><li><strong>处理器:</strong> Quad Core i5 / Ryzen 5 or better<br></li><li><strong>内存:</strong> 8 GB RAM<br></li><li><strong>显卡:</strong> GTX 1060 / RX 580 or better<br></li><li><strong>DirectX 版本:</strong> 11<br></li><li><strong>网络:</strong> 宽带互联网连接<br></li><li><strong>存储空间:</strong> 需要 2 GB 可用空间<br></li><li><strong>支持 VR:</strong> SteamVR<br></li><li><strong>附注事项:</strong> Content will need to be downloaded to local disk. Additional disk space will be required.</li></ul>							</ul>
						</div>

					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 5,168.3 小时												（评测时 1,588.8 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，ChilloutVR 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary123497068_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2022 年 10 月 8 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 序列号													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					<b>您好，如果您是一名初来乍到的ChilloutVR玩家，可以加入开发者认证中文社区𝐐𝐐群: 𝟯𝟰𝟳𝟰𝟵𝟰𝟵𝟮𝟰 。</b><br><b>在写下这篇评测时，我已经将我在VRChat中所有的地图创作全部删除，部分被迁移至ChilloutVR平台，VRChat现在已有离线VRCW Rip的功能，我实在无法放心我的原创内容在VRChat中受到非法盗窃，所以我选择相信更为安全的Alpha Blend Interactive。</b><br><b> Bye VRChat Inc. , say hello to Alpha Blend Interactive. </b><br>=============================================================<br>    首先，我想要给ChilloutVR的CEO兼网络API开发者 Marmeladensalat 一个诚挚的道谢，是你对玩家的态度让我决定为ABI输出独家原创内容并创立中文社区。作为一名来自德国的开发者，愿意和远在东方的华人玩家进行深度沟通，甚至创建QQ账号加入群聊，我认为一个开发者能有这样谦虚的行为，是一种难得可贵的品质体现。<br>    简单来评价一下这段时间在ChilloutVR中游玩后的感觉。<br>    1.优化方面好过VRChat太多，同样的双平台地图，ChilloutVR甚至能在相同占用的情况下高出VRChat 30-50FPS，人多时也不会出现10FPS的折磨体验，40人同时在线的Jazz Club依然能够在RTX2060/RTX3090下获得40/90FPS的优秀帧数表现。<br>    2.内容输出更为纯净，能够很轻松避开VRChat的烂梗人，也能够随着时间沉淀出一部分真正热爱的玩家，过滤掉跟风游玩的人。<br>    3.开发者对华人态度十分友好亲近，每一个中文社区的稳定玩家都能够拿出实质性证据来证实此观点并非空穴来风。我们和CEO:Marmeladensalat在中秋节时举办了一场中秋派对+TA的生日派对，为TA做了一个虚拟蛋糕，这或许是我们这些玩家能够做的全部了。<br>    4.华人社区已经成型，每天有一定数量的华人玩家活跃在社区中以及游戏内，为初来乍到的华人玩家指明道路，为这个用心建立起的社区维护秩序。<br>    5.ChilloutVR的SDK: CCK 相较于VRC Udon SDK要拥有更多基础便利性，开关、本地、全局同步、Instance Owner Only、传送、双质量镜子、区域Trigger等大量的脚本是预设好的，只需要在CCK内设置即可，告别繁琐复杂的Udon Graph/Sharp，但缺点同样存在，相较于Udon损失了部分上限，无法编写出非常复杂的脚本，但对于初学者或业余者来说，CCK的使用体验远高于VRC Udon SDK。<br>    6.Mod的开放性极高，但官方也同时在不安装反作弊的情况下限制了恶性Mod的使用，促使目前ChilloutVR的Mod几乎全部为优化类的良性Mod，包括汉化Mod，界面优化Mod。<br>    7.开发者已经保证将官方双语汉化(简体/繁体)加入更新计划表(After R171~R172)，未来将支持官方中文。<br>=======================================================================================<br><br>目前我是ChilloutVR的第一个中国Moderator，有了本地化的Moderator，对社区的管理和扶持会更加便利，也更能防止社区文化走向畸形，合理输出正面文化反馈。<br>诚挚地邀请所有内容创作者入驻ChilloutVR，已有中文流ChilloutVR世界建造教程，链接：𝗵𝘁𝘁𝗽𝘀://𝘄𝘄𝘄.𝗯𝗶𝗹𝗶𝗯𝗶𝗹𝗶.𝗰𝗼𝗺/𝘃𝗶𝗱𝗲𝗼/𝗕𝗩𝟭𝗲𝗡𝟰𝘆𝟭𝗡𝟳𝗙𝟰/<br>以上。<br>                 -ChilloutVR Project 12 【十二场梦】系列地图总负责人，Alpha Blend Interactive Discord Chat Mod<br>                       -代表华人设计师  Alpha Blend Interactive Volunteer Contributing.<br>                              - Bby Kairi.   2022/10/8					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>
